</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International Highlights Progress on Focused </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Growth Strategy through Accelerated Marketing&nbsp;&amp; Sales at </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>2023 CAGNY Conference </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Marketing and Sales transformation powering growth in core categories with iconic brands including <I>Oreo, Ritz,
LU, Clif Bar</I> and <I>Tate&#146;s Bake Shop</I> biscuits and baked snacks, as well as <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk, Milka</I> and <I>Toblerone</I> chocolate </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Personalized, digital approach enabling deeper consumer and customer connectivity in both developed and emerging
markets </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>CHICAGO &#150; February</B><B>&nbsp;21, 2023</B><B> &#150; </B>Mondel&#275;z International (Nasdaq: MDLZ) today will
highlight how its higher-growth, more focused portfolio is benefiting from accelerated marketing and sales at the 2023 Consumer Analyst Group of New York (CAGNY) Conference. Chairman and Chief Executive Officer Dirk Van de Put, Chief Financial
Officer Luca Zaramella, and Chief Marketing and Sales Officer Martin Renaud will detail the Company&#146;s progress in delivering strong, sustainable growth in core categories; improving commercial operations and performance; and reshaping its
portfolio through growth-accretive acquisitions.<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We&#146;re excited to showcase how our marketing and sales transformation is advancing our
focused growth strategy, as well as highlighting the latest developments in our portfolio reshaping plan,&#148; Van de Put said. &#147;By focusing on profit dollar growth, local-first commercial execution, high-return investment and clearly defined
incentives, we have step-changed the company&#146;s trajectory, and we are approaching the next phase of our evolution with acceleration and focus.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Showing Progress Against Our Strategy </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z
International has reinvented its marketing and sales strategy in the last few years, resulting in strong growth, increased efficiency and improved productivity &#150; enabling the Company to further invest in its widely loved brands. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We have shifted our investment posture in recent years to higher levels of spending supporting a more
focused portfolio of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">purpose-led</FONT> brands, and it&#146;s clear this strategy is paying off,&#148; Renaud said. &#147;Our marketing and sales transformation has enabled us to demonstrate strong positions in our
core categories, driving demand and growing brand loyalty to advance further growth while strengthening cultural relevance in both emerging and developed markets.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The presentation will focus on three key areas of Mondel&#275;z International&#146;s strategy to drive sustainable long-term growth: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

biscuits and baked snacks </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Simultaneous with the webcast for CAGNY participants, today&#146;s presentation and accompanying slides will be available in the investor section of the
Company&#146;s website (<U>www.mondelezinternational.com</U>) and will remain available on the website following the webcast. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Mondel&#275;z
International </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) empowers people to snack right in over 150 countries around the world. With 2022 net
revenues of approximately $31&nbsp;billion, MDLZ is leading the future of snacking with iconic global and local brands such as <I>Oreo, Ritz, LU, Clif Bar</I> and <I>Tate&#146;s Bake Shop</I> biscuits and baked snacks, as well as <I>Cadbury Dairy
Milk, Milka</I> and <I>Toblerone</I> chocolate. Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#146;s 500, Nasdaq 100 and Dow Jones Sustainability Index. Visit <U>www.mondelezinternational.com</U> or follow the company on
Twitter at <U>www.twitter.com/MDLZ</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></P>
